import "sampledata"
import "experimental"
import "experimental/aggregate"

left = from(bucket: "jmeter_night")
|> range(start: experimental.subDuration(from: now(), d: 48h), stop: experimental.subDuration(from: now(), d: 24h))
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_measurement"] == "jmeter")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["application"] == "myApplication")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_field"] == "pct95.0")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["transaction"] == "all")
|> group(columns: ["transaction"])
|> aggregateWindow(every: 10m, fn: mean)
|> timeShift(duration: 24h, columns: ["_start", "_stop", "_time"])
|> yield(name: "left")

right = from(bucket: "jmeter_night")
|> range(start: experimental.subDuration(from: now(), d: 24h), stop: now())
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_measurement"] == "jmeter")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["application"] == "myApplication")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_field"] == "pct95.0")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["transaction"] == "all")
|> group(columns: ["transaction"])
|> aggregateWindow(every: 10m, fn: mean)
|> yield(name: "right")

–ü–æ–¥—Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–∏ –º–Ω–µ –≤ influx community –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç —Ä–∞–±–æ—á–∏–π: 

 
yesterday = 
    from(bucket: "jmeter_night") 
        |> range(start: -48h, stop: -24h) 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["_measurement"] == "jmeter") 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["application"] == "my application") 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["_field"] == "pct95.0") 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["transaction"] == "all") 
        |> aggregateWindow(every: 10m, fn: mean) 
        |> timeShift(duration: 24h) 
        |> set(key: "day", value: "yesterday") 
        |> group(columns: ["_time", "_value"], mode: "except") 
 
today = 
    from(bucket: "jmeter_night") 
        |> range(start: -24h) 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["_measurement"] == "jmeter") 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["application"] == "my application") 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["_field"] == "pct95.0") 
        |> filter(fn: (r) => r["transaction"] == "all") 
        |> aggregateWindow(every: 10m, fn: mean) 
        |> set(key: "day", value: "today") 
        |> group(columns: ["_time", "_value"], mode: "except") 
 
union(tables: [yesterday, today]) 
    |> pivot(rowKey: ["_time"], columnKey: ["day"], valueColumn: "_value") 
    |> map(fn: (r) => ({r with _value: r.today - r.yesterday}))

1. install brew install influxdb-cli –∏–ª–∏ –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–± —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∏ influxdb-cli
2. Open http://influxdbHostName:8086/
3. Menu / Load Data / Buckets -> Create Bucket
4. Name of bucket: k6, retention of bucket: Forever, id: 111111111111 (smthx)
5. Get Token and orgID: Menu / About / OrgId : 222222222222
6. Map InfluxDB 2 bucket to InfluxDB 1 database via HTTP Request:

curl --request POST http://influxdbHostName:8086/api/v2/dbrps \
  --header "Authorization: Token ...token..." \
  --header 'Content-type: application/json' \
  --data '{"bucketID": "111111111111", "database": "k6", "default": false, "orgID": "222222222222", "retention_policy": "auto" }'

7. Create an influxdb user:
influx v1 auth create \
--host http://influxdbHostName:8086 \
--token ...token... \
--org-id 222222222222 \
--read-bucket 111111111111 \
--write-bucket 111111111111 \
--username loginForK6
